FOREWORD~-------------,  At the beginning of the World War, with European sources  cut off, the need for high grade laboratory glassware in  this country was most urgent. When chemists and Govern- ment officials sought our assistance, we were fortunate,  thanks to our research staff, in having a glass possessing  ideal properties for use in the manufacture of laboratory  ware.  Although the glass was available, we had little experience  in fabricating it into the many shapes and to the exacting  specifications required for chemical work. With the con- stant help, advice and constructive criticism of American  chemists, we have been able to make definite progress each  year in perfecting "PYREX" brand laboratory glassware,  now generally accepted as standard throughout the world.  We pledge the continuance of our efforts to improve the  quality and usefulness of our products, and trust we may  merit the continued support and good will of our chemist  friends.  This  new and more complete catalog is offered for your  approval and use, with sincere appreciation of the fine  cooperation and assistance accorded us down through the  years.  
'1'. RE-"'  ~· v.  PYREX  (, «·  ·.s_IJAT.o«  THE ''PYREX'' TRADE-MARK AND  ITS SIGNIFICANCE  E VERY piece of "PYREX" brand laboratory glassware is distinctly marked with the circular trade- mark shown above. Since this trade-mark appears only on products manufactured completely  by Corning Glass Works, it enables the user to identify Corning manufactured and fabricated  laboratory glassware.  Corning Glass Works manufactures only one grade of laboratory glassware. Every piece of ware  bearing our "PYREX" trade-mark must conform to the high standards of quality as established,  maintained, and consistently improved by Corning through years of practical experience and scien- tific research.  The attention of chemists is directed to the following important factors contributing to the uniformity,  high quality, and dependability of laboratory glassware bearing our trade-mark:  •Made from "PYREX" brand chemical glass-a glass of high chemical durability and low  expansion.  •Blown and fabricated by expert workmen thoroughly trained and long skilled in the art of  manipulating low expansion glasses.  •Annealed in continuous belt type lehrs designed to insure uniform results and used exclu- sively for "PYREX" brand glasses.  • Laboratory control exercised over all phases of the production routine from raw materials  to finished product.  Modern laboratory technique requires glassware in which high mechanical strength is combined  with maximum thermal and chemical resistance. These essential requirements are characteristic of  " PYREX" brand chemical glass. Of equal importance is the character of the workmanship and the  annealing. For this reason, we can assume responsibility only for laboratory glassware bearing our  "PYREX" trade-mark which denotes manufacture in finished form by Corning Glass Works.  
IMPORTANT PROPERTIES  of "Pyrex" Brand Chemical Glass ________  1  In presenting this latest edition of our "PYREX LABOMTORY GLASSWARE" catalog, we  wish to emphasize again certain physical and chemical characteristics of "PYREX" brand  chemical glass that are of major importance in their contribution to the economy, accuracy,  and durability of the glassware as well as to the safety and satisfaction of the user.  LOW EXPANSION  An extremely low thermal expansion coefficient (0.0000032 be- tween 19-350 degrees C .)  minimizes losses from thermal shock and  also permits heavy, rugged construction, thereby increasing the re- sistance to mechanical breakage. The result is greater safety to the  laboratory worker and economies in ultimate glassware costs.  LOW ALKALI CHARACTERISTICS  Particular a ttention is invited to the low alkali characteristic and the  high chemical durability of "PYREX" brand chemical glass. (See  Chemical  Durability Tests-Technical Data, page 5 .) The amount  of glass dissolved by preparations made or stored in "PYREX" brand  glassware is so small (by virtue of the extremely low solubility of the  glass from which this ware is made) that the technician may rest  assured that the hydrogen ion concentration of his material will not  be appreciably altered. Accuracy-the foundation of laboratory  technique-is thereby safeguarded insofar as laboratory glassware  is concerned.  ST ABILITY IN STERILIZATION  For either hot air (dry) or steam (wet) sterilization, "PYREX" glassware  is unequalled. It is not affected thermally or chemically by any of the  methods commonly employe d in laboratories where sterilization is a  major factor in routine or specialized work. Actual tests have shown  that "PYREX" glassware remains clear after more than twenty  w shings with a 5~ solution of Na aPO ,, and allowed to dry partially  without rinsing before each sterilization.  
TECHNICAL DATA  "PYREX" is a trade-mark identifying various  resistant glasses and glass products made by  Corning Glass Works. The many "PYREX"  brand glasses developed by Corning offer a  wide range of physical and chemical proper- ties from which to select glassware suitable for  any specific application.  Unless otherwise indicated, the items listed in  this catalog are fabricated from "PYREX"  brand chemical glass No. 774. Careful con- sideration of the following characteristics will  show that this particular "PYREX" brand glass  is best suited for all general laboratory work.  Composition-The simple chemical composi- tion of "PYREX" brand chemical glass used in the  manufacture of laboratory ware is advantageous  in minimizing contamination of the liquids in  contact with it. It is a borosilicate glass having  low alkali content. It contains no elements of the  magnesia-lime-zinc group and no heavy metals.  Chemical Durability-Some idea of the dura- bility of "PYREX" brand chemical glass may be  obtained from the following information:  Loss in weight, redistilled water-48 hrs. at  80°C.-.000002 grams per sq. cm.  Loss in weight, 100 lbs. steam pressure for 96  hours-.0005 grams per sq. cm.  Loss in weight, boiling 6 hours in 5 3 NaOH-
.002 grams per sq. cm.  Loss  in weight, 5 3 HCL for 72 hours at 80°C.  -.000002 grams per sq. cm.  The above representative figures are given as a  guide. The solubility of glass is influenced by so  many variables that the only safe way to com- pare two glasses is to test them simultaneously.  By such tests the superior resistance of "PYREX"  brand chemical glass is readily demonstrated.  Softening Point-Glass has no definite soften- ing point but arbitrarily the softening point is  defined as the temperature at which a glass rod  1 mm in diameter and 150 mm in length will  elongate under its own weight, when suspended  vertically, at the rate of 1 mm per minute. For  "PYREX" brand chemical glass the "softening  point" value is approximately 820 degrees C .  5  Temperature Limits in Service-In general,  it is safe to assume that a glass will be sufficiently  viscous to withstand deformation when heated  to its annealing temperature. In cases of long  time heating, or when the glass is subject to  pressure, the strain point is the highest safe  operating temperature. For "PYREX" brand  chemical glass the annealing point is 560 de- grees C. and the strain point is 510 degrees C.  For some shapes, and for a relatively short time,  this glass can be heated above 600 degrees C.  When properly supported and not under high  internal pressure satisfactory service has been  obtained at higher temperatures, but it should  be understood that any glass, when heated  above its strain point temperature and then  quickly cooled, will acquire strains which may  affect its later serviceability.* However, if pre- caution is taken to cool the glass slowly and  uniformly after such heating, reannealing will  take place and thus reduce the danger of in- duced strain.  OTHER PHYSICAL DATA ON  "PYREX" BRAND CHEMICAL GLASS  Specific Gravity-2.23  Specific Heat-0.20 gm. cals. per gm. degree  Elasticity Coefficient-6900 Kg. per sq. mm.  Thermal Conductivity-0.0027 cal. per cm.  cube (cm 2 /cm) per degree C .  Linear Coefficient of Expansion-.0000032 be- tween 19-350 degrees C.  Refractive Index-Sodium (D Line) 1.474  Light Transmission-923 in 2 mm thickness;  90.53 in 5 mm thickness  *See Littleton & Dasney article-"Extending the Life of  Chemical Glassware." Industrial & Engineering Chem- istry, Vol. 19, Nov. 1927, page 1271. Reprints of this  article  will be sent on request.  
6  11 PYREX 11  BRAND LABORATORY GLASSWARE  GENERAL INFORMATION-DIRECTIONS FOR ORDERING  It is suggested that users of this catalog read this page carefully.  PRICES-All prices shown in the catalog  are consumer's net prices. Discounts for  single original package quantities and dis- counts for quantity orders of 20, 50 and 100 or  more original packages have already been  calculated and all prices shown are net.  DEFINITION OF "ORIGINAL PACK- AGES" -Original packages, referred to simply  as "packages" in this catalog, are those con- taining the indicated number of pieces of only  one type and one size of ware as manufactured,  trade-marked, and packed by Corning Glass  Works.  QUANTITY DISCOUNTS-(A) Quantity dis- counts now apply to practically all items in both  Parts I and II of this catalog. The only exceptions  are a few items in Part II which are packed one  piece per package. In every instance these items  are identified by the notation "not subject to  quantity discounts nor to be included as a  com- ponent part of 20, 50 and 100 case orders.''  (B) Quantity discounts apply only to the specific  items of " PYREX" brand laboratory ware as  listed and described in this catalog, and only  when ordered in full original package quantities.  (C) To  secure quantity prices as shown under  the headings:  "Net price per package in assortments of 20  pkgs."-i.e., for quantities of from 20  to 49 original packages.  " Net price per package in assortments of 50  pkgs."-i.e., for quantities of from 50  to 99 original packages.  "Net price per package in assortments of  100 pkgs."-i.e., for quantities of 100  or more original packages.  it is  required that delivery of the entire order be  made at one time and to one destination.  (D)  Assortments: Quantity prices, as indicated  above, are applicable to assortments of ware  containing the requisite number of cases, pro- vided full original package quantities of each  individual item are ordered. For example, in  making up a 20 case order, as many as 20  separate items may be included, if full original  package quantities of each item are specified in  every instance.  (E) Irrespective of the number of original pack- ages ordered, any additional pieces which may  be included, if less than an original package  quantity for that item, take "net price each"  prices as listed in the catalog and are not sub- ject to any discount.  (F) In order to obtain the full benefit of quantity  prices and for convenience in handling,   it is  suggested that customers state their requirements  so far as possible in units of original package  quantities or exact multiples thereof and not as  single pieces.  *  *  *  *  HOW TO ORDER-Please give catalog num- ber and type together with capacity or dimen- sions as shown, or code word.  WHERE TO ORDER-All items listed may be  obtained from dealers in laboratory supplies  throughout the country or from Corning Glass  Works at prices shown.  All shipments made direct from the factory are  f.o.b . Corning, packages charged extra.  TERMS-Thirty days net, or net payment on  the 25th proximo.  SPECIAL APPARATUS (not shown in  catalog)-We solicit direct inquiries from cus- tomers for special apparatus to be made of  "PYREX" brand chemical glass. Our technical  staff will be glad to cooperate in designing and  developing new apparatus for unusual require- ments.  Corning Glass Works • Laboratory and Pharmaceutical Division • Corning, New York

In Assortments of  20 50 100  Pkgs. Pkgs. Pkgs.  This all glass two piece "PYREX" cell withstands both repeated sterilization  and the use of acid cleaning solutions.  In practice, the top section (dimensions 38 x 38 x 1 mm thick) having fine  ground surface and a 20 mm center opening, is placed on the polished bottom  plate (dimensions 37 x 60 x 2 mm thick) and a tight seal is obtained between the  two parts if the surfaces are wet. 33  "PYREX" Brand DESICCATORS  The design of "PYREX" Desiccator covers and bodies has been modified to reduce the tendency to collapse  under reduced pressures sometimes encountered in desiccators of older design. Each complete desiccator is  tested under vacuum for twenty-four hours, and a minimum twenty-inch mercury manometer reading after  the prescribed time limit is incorporated in our manufacturing specifications. The varying service conditions  encountered in vacuum work are such as to make it impossible to guarantee desiccators against breakage.  An improved method of flat grinding permits interchangeability of lids and bodies on "PYREX" Desiccators,  and the separate parts are accordingly listed below. "PYREX" Brand  EXTRACTORS AND  EXTRACTION APPARATUS  "PYREX" Brand Extraction Apparatus is  of  rugged construction throughout. Most  ground joint models are made with ground  zone on condenser jacket so that the con- denser itself hts directly into the extractor.  The water cooled joint thus provided,  eliminates the use of sealed-on condenser  joints enabling us to offer a more compact  apparatus of reduced height and increased  efficiency.  All  ground joints are interchangeable and  are made in strict accordance with Com- mercial Standards CS 21-36 of the National  Bureau of Standards.  Flasks, Extractors, or  Condensers may be ordered separately  with the assurance that they  will be inter- changeable with any previously purchased  Corning Glass Works Extraction Appara- tus bearing the Standard Taper (T) mark- i ng.  8 THE MARK OF CORNING CRAFTSMANSHIP 8  r

"PYREX" Brand DISTILLING FLASKS  In the petroleum products testing laboratory, fire hazards may be reduced to a minimum through the use  of "PYREX" Brand Laboratory Ware. The distillation of volatile materials requires that the utmost precaution  be taken to eliminate all possible danger of fire and explosion which may result from the use of inferior glass- ware.  We recommend the use of "PYREX" Distilling Flasks for all distillation work, and more particularly for the  distillation of highly volatile or flammable products as encountered in A.S.T.M. 64  "PYREX" Brand KJELDAHL FLASKS  "PYREX" Kjeldahl Flasks, because of their physical and chemical properties have become the accepted  standard in fertilizer, cereal and other industries. A low coefficient of expansion combined with high chemical  stability enables "PYREX" Kjeldahl Flasks to successfully meet the severe conditions encountered in nitrogen  digestions and distillations. 66  "PYREX" Brand VOLUMETRIC FLASKS  "PYREX" Volumetric Flasks, because of their sturdiness, accuracy and quality of workmanship, are recom- mended for all general purposes, and particularly where a glass of high chemical stability and resistance to  heat shock is required. All "PYREX" Volumetric Flasks are calibrated on the basis of the metric liter, i . e., the  unit of capacity equivalent to the volume occupied by the mass of 1 kilogram of pure water at its maximum  density (4° C. practically).  Our standard "PYREX" Volumetric ware, unless otherwise specified, is calibrated to contain at 20° C., and  is held to twice the tolerance prescribed by the National Bureau of Standards for certified ware. (See circular  No. 9, National Bureau of Standards "Testing of Glass Volumetric Apparatus," also Federal Specification  DD-V-581.)  Corning Certified "PYREX" Volumetric ware is held within the tolerance and specifications prescribed by  the National Bureau of Standards. Each piece is accompanied by a Corning Certificate, the number of which  corresponds to the number appearing in the rectangle just below the "C" on each piece of ware. 76  "PYREX" Brand PHARMACEUTICAL GRADUATES  "PYREX" Pharmaceutical Graduates, because of the extremely low thermal coefficient of expansion of the  glass from which they are constructed, oiler the maximum in thermal resistance. They can be repeatedly  sterilized without clouding. The low coefficient of expansion also permits heavy wall construction throughout,  thereby giving greater mechanical strength than is possible with higher expansion glasses.  "PYREX" Graduates are calibrated and acid etched in accordance with specifications of the National Bureau  of Standards, and the latest edition of U. S. Pharmacopoeia. They may be used legally in all states and terri- tories of the United States.  All  numbered graduations completely encircle the graduate and the shortest lines extend one-fourth the  distance around the graduate. Two styles of graduations are listed. No. 6500 has single scale and is gradu- ated in fluid ounces. No. 6520 has double scale and is graduated in both fluid ounces and in milliliters  Quan- Net  NET PRICE PER PKG. STANDARD TAPER (T) INTERCHANGEABLE  GROUND JOINTS  SPECIFICATIONS AND DESIGNATIONS  The development of interchangeable ground  joints has progressed steadily since their general  introduction a few years ago. Their general  utility, economy, and convenience have been  definitely established.  New Designations, Types, Sizes-The  National Bureau of Standards, through its Com- mittee on Interchangeable Ground Joints (see  Commercial Standards CS 21-36), has introduced  a new series of Medium Length Joints; also two  new sizes in Standard Full Lengths. This has  FULL LENGTH JOINTS  made necessary a new method of designation,  consisting of two figures, the first indicating the  approximate diameter (in millimeters) at the  large end, the second giving the length of  ground glass zone. Thus T 5 /20 indicates a  ground zone 5 mm in diameter at the large end,  and 20 mm in length. For purposes of com- parison, old and new designations for full length  joints, and the designations used for medium  length joints are shown below:  MEDIUM LENGTH JOINTS  (Taper, 1  to 10; i.e., one mm ± 0 .006 mm per centimeter of length on diameter)  New  t Old  Designation Computed  Designation Computed  Designation (Large  Diam.  Approx.  (Large Diam. Approx.  (Approx.  Diam./Length  Large End Length Diam./Length  Large End Length  Diam. of  Ground  of Ground of Ground  of Ground of Ground of Ground  Small End) Zone)  Zone  Zone  Zone) Zone Zone  mm  mm mm mm  mm mm  mm  3  5 /20  5.0  20  " 5 / 12  5.0 12  5 7 / 25  7.5  25  " 7 / 15  7 .5 15  7  10/30  10.0 30  "10/ 18  10.0  18  9 12/30  12.0 30  " 12/ 18  12.0  18  11  14/35  14.5  35 " 14/20  14.5 20  15  19/38  18.8  38 " 19/22  18.8 22  20  24 /40  24.0  40 "24/25  24.0 25  25  29 /42  29.2  42  "29/26  29.2 26  30  34/45  34.5  45  "34/28  34.5 28  "35 40/50  40.0  50  "40/35  40.0 35  40  45 /50  45.0  50  50  55 /50  55.0  50  "55  60/50  60.0  50  65 71/60  71.0  60  " Newly introduced ground joints.  t The old  designation also served to denote the approximate outside diameter of the straight section of tubing forming a part  of each joint member.  For example,  the straight sections of tubing on T 5 /20 (old designation T 3) and on T 5 / 12 joints  are approximately 3  mm O .D . for sealing to tubing of this diameter.  77  
78  "PYREX" Brand STANDARD TAPER(T)INTERCHANGEABLE  GROUND JOINTS  As early as 1919, in collaboration with a  manufacturer of physical apparatus, we fabri- cated interchangeable ground joints for use on a  "PYREX" mercury vapor pump. The experience  gained and the technique developed since that  time, together with modern precision grinding  equipment, enable us to offer a definitely  improved product.  "PYREX" brand T joints are:  ACCURATE-They are made in strict accord- ance with the requirements and specifications  of the National Bureau of Standards. To  insure this result, our grinding tools are made  to precision limits-and are reconditioned as  frequently as required to compensate for  wear.  DURABLE-The walls are uniform and sturdy.  The outer member has a heavy beaded end,  the inner member a firepolished end finish.  All parts are thoroughly annealed in accu- rately controlled lehrs designed exclusively  for annealing "PYREX" brand glassware.  UNIFORM IN QUALITY-Every joint mem- ber is stamped with this trade-mark e-your  definite assurance that the part is made of  "PYREX" brand chemical glass, and that it  has been completely fabricated in the appa- ratus shop of Corning Glass Works.  Every size of T ground joint approved by the  National Bureau of Standards (see "Commercial  Standard CS2 l-36") is listed in this catalog, and  each part of the joint is marked with the symbol  "T" to indicate standard taper ware. With a  few minor exceptions, all joints, stoppers, con- necting tubes, and other ware with ground sur- faces, listed in this catalog, are interchangeable,  conform with standard taper specifications, and  bear the symbol "T".  Although several hundred adaptations of this  feature could have been included, we have  catalogued only the more commonly used items.  Our facilities for the design and fabrication of  glassware with "PYREX" brand T ground joints  are always available to customers requiring  special apparatus. Inquiries are solicited.  Shop assembly of " PYREX" apparatus with Tparts. Designed for esterification of chaulmoogra oil used in treatment of leprosy.  This  apparatus was manufactured for shipment to South America.

50 23.40  "PYREX" Brand PIPETTES  $12.65 $11.99 $11.32  17.96 17.01 16.07  22.23 21.06 19.89  "PYREX" Pipettes will withstand repeated sterilization (wet or dry). They are affected neither chemically  nor thermally by any of the methods commonly employed in laboratories where sterilization is a major factor  in routine or in specialized work.  These Pipettes are made with walls of proper thickness for maximum mechanical strength and convenient  handling. The tips have a gradual taper and are stone finished to avoid any sudden constriction at the orifice.  The Measuring and Volumetric types conform in design with the specifications as outlined in Circular No. 9  of the National Bureau of Standards. The Measuring and Serological types comform in design with Federal  Specifications DD-V-581. "PYREX" STOPCOCKS  c THE MARK OF CORNING CRAITSMANSHIP ~  v v  
89  "PYREX" Brand STOPCOCKS  "PYREX" Stopcocks are recommended for use in the construction of all special designs of research appara- tus. They are of heavy construction throughout. Mechanical strength is further increased in sealing on the  side arms by thoroughly reworking the glass so as to obtain a heavy reinforced seal.  "PYREX" Stopcocks are furnished with solid moulded stoppers, and the trade-mark "PYREX" is pressed  into the handle of each piece. The stoppers are of the same composition and expansion coefficient as the  shell, thereby reducing danger of leakage and freezing due to temperature changes. In case solid stoppers  stick in the barrel of the stopcocks, they can ordinarily be loosened by mechanical removers designed for  this purpose, whereas hollow stoppers are likely to be crushed under this treatment.  "PYREX" Standard Stopcocks are ground by improved methods made possible by enlarged manufacturing  facilities, thus assuring higher quality than heretofore obtainable. They are satisfactory for all general  vacuum work. If other than standard stopcocks are required for unusual applications, they will be supplied  to order, and this individual grinding treatment will necessitate a slight price increase. All standard stopcocks  (with the exception of micro and mercury seal types) are grooved at the lower end of the stopper and are  supplied with rubber washers to prevent stoppers' dropping out.  All straight bore stopcocks (except catalog No. 7320) are now made to conform strictly to the Standard  Taper specifications outlined in National Bureau of Standards Bulletin CS2 l-36. Since several different  sized bores may be drilled through any given size of stopper, the approved method of designating size of  T Stopcock Stoppers is by bore diameter only.  Approx. Stop- Approx. Attention is called to the following statement appearing under Paragraph 11,  Pg. 4, in Bulletin CS21-36 of the National Bureau of Standards. "Interchange- able ground glass stopcocks are not intended for vacuum apparatus or for use  with light liquids. When it becomes necessary to replace a plug of an inter- changeable stopcock which, by constant abrasion, has become worn so that the  shell is enlarged while the plug is diminished in size or otherwise physically or  chemically acted upon, then interchangeable stopcock plugs cannot be expect- ed to fit properly in the shell." The illustration will indicate the basic principle of this tube which is made  from "PYREX" Brand Chemical Glass Tubing with a  solid partition through the  center. The lower end of the partition does not extend to the bottom of the tube  in order to leave a communicating opening between the sides. Near the top of  the tube on opposite sides of the partition are two side tubulations which can be  connected to other apparatus. Where desirable to first absorb C02, then  moisture, one side of the tube can be filled with Ascarite, the other side with  Anhydrone. It can, of course,  also be used with other granular drying chemi- cals such as Calcium Chloride, Dehydrite, etc.  FEAOK *20xl50 12 $2.00 $21.60 $20.52 $19.44 $18.36  *Suitable for microchemical applications. 103  "PYREX" Brand COMBUSTION TUBES  While not originally developed for combustion work, Combustion Tubing made from "PYREX" Brand  Chemical Glass is satisfactory where temperatures above 750 degrees Centigrade are not required. For  continued use at a maximum temperature of 500 degrees Centigrade, or for short periods at 750 degrees  Centigrade, we recommend the use of our catalog items Nos. 8600 and 8620, "PYREX" Combustion Tubes.  In order to meet the need for Combustion Tubes where higher temperatures are involved, we offer a new  hard, resistant tube made from "PYREX" Brand Ignition Tube glass No. 172. This glass has been developed  for use in the manufacture of Combustion and Ignition Tubes, high temperature thermometers, and other  similar purposes, and has a linear coefficient of expansion of .0000039 between 19-350 degrees Centigrade.  The softening point is 925 degrees Centigrade, this being the temperature at which a glass rod 1 mm in diam- eter, suspended vertically, elongates of its own weight at the rate of 1 mm per minute. Combustion tubing  from this glass is satisfactory for temperatures as high as 850 degrees Centigrade for short periods, and for  temperatures as high as 675 degrees Centigrade for continued use.  Combustion Tubes of "PYREX" Brand Glass No. 172 are listed under catalog items Nos. 8560,  8580,  8660, 8680, 8700, and 8720.  Combustion Tubes made from "PYREX" Brand Chemical Glass are listed under Nos. 8600, 8620, and 8640.  Quan- Net NET PRICE PER PKG.  Number  and Type  Approx. "PYREX" Brand STANDARD TAPER ('f) ADAPTER,  CONNECTING, AND DISTILLING TUBES  From the innumerable possible combinations of inner and outer joint members, only the most widely used  sizes and shapes of adapter, connecting, and distilling tubes have been selected for listing as standard in this  catalog. 30  $32.40  15.12  14.04  12.96  $30.78 $29.16 $27.54  14.36 13.61 12.85  13.34 12.64 11.93  12.31 11.66  11.02  "PYREX" Brand TEST AND CULTURE TUBES  At the new prices "PYREX" Test and Culture Tubes are the most economical tubes available. They are  made from selected machine made tubing of correct wall weight. They are well annealed, strong mechani- cally, highly resistant to heat, and chemically stable.  Comparative tests under normal service conditions, as conducted by many educational users, prove con- clusively that "PYREX" Test Tubes are the most enduring tubes obtainable. Carefully kept records of these  service tests show definitely that very substantial savings can be effected through less breakage and a resultant  reduction in yearly replacement costs by standardizin g on "PYREX" Test Tubes.  "PYREX" Culture Tubes are particularly suited for use in bacteriological work, as repeated sterilization,  either wet or dry, does not cause clouding. Because of the relatively low alkali content, together with the  high chemical stability of the glass, the pH of media is not appreciably affected, even if left in "PYREX" Culture  Tubes for long periods of time. The uniform, substantial walls result in reduced breakage both in use and in  washing.  "PYREX" Test and Culture Tubes are packed in compact, sealed-sleeve type cardboard containers, each  holding twelve tubes. This method of packing gives utmost protection in shipping, convenience in handling,  and cleanliness. Pk gs.  $10.37 $ 9.85 $   9.33 $   8.81  11.66  11.08  10.50 9 .91  12.96 12.31  11.66 11.02  17.50 16.62 15.75 14.87  26.24 24.93 23.62 22.31  ROD  Because of the ease with which "PYREX" Brand Tubing can be manipulated before the blast lamp, and its  comparatively wide working range, it is particularly adapted for use by the beginnerin laboratory glassblowing.  An instructive booklet on the manipulation of "PYREX" Brand Tubing will be supplied free on request.  For the scientist or laboratory glassblower, "PYREX" Tubing otters numerous distinct advantages. In the  construction and repair of laboratory apparatus it is necessary to employ tubing having the same physical  characteristics as the glass from which the apparatus was originally made. Otherwise, unnecessary strains, set  up because of lack of uniformity in composition and expansion, may result in subsequent breakage. "PYREX"  Brand Tubing is identical in composition and physical characteristics with "PYREX" Brand Chemical Ware.  In the construction of special apparatus, much labor can be saved by utilizing "PYREX" Brand Tubing  together with standard blanks (Flasks, Stopcocks, T Ground Joints, T Connecting Tubes, etc.), and attention is  called to the wide selection of such blanks appearin g throughout this catalog. 119  PART II  The following items of "PYREX" Brand Chemical Glass are made for Industrial and Pharmaceutical manu- facturers. While not primarily intended for laboratory use, they will be found convenient for many purposes.  They are not suitable for pressure or vacuum work, and should not be subjected to direct contact with the  heat source.  Items  pressed or blown with heavy walls may have marks in the body, such as cords and shear marks.  Such marks are incidental to the character of the glass and process of manufacture, and are not to be con- sidered as defects or in any way detrimental to the use of the ware. FIBROUS GLASS  121  FIBROUS GLASS  We offer two types of glass Fibre (Wool), both made especially for laboratory filtration work. Manufactured  by glass tank methods, the fibres are of near microscopic fineness (diameter about 0.0002" to 0 .0003" ) and  are strong, resilient, soft, and pliable.  Although both types are identical in physical characteristics, "PYREX" Brand Fibrous Glass No. 719 is  superior in chemical durability.  These two items are supplied in the form of sheets about .Vs" thick by 10" wide, and are wrapped in con- venient half-pound rolls. Not sold in quantities of less than 1  roll (one-half pound). CORNING GLASS WORKS  CORN INC, NEW YORK  LABOllATOBY & PHAIIMACEUTICAL DIVISION'  August 1 5 , 1938  TO USERS OF LABORA.'l'ORY GLASSWARE  We are pleased to present herewith catalog No. LP-18, superseding all previous is- sues, as well as all supplements and pamphlets on "PYREX" brand laboratory g1assware.  This is by far the most comprehensive catalog we have o ffered. Within its 1 28  pages will be f ound 2353 individual items, 737 of which have not been listed previously.  From  the many advances made in the field of glass laboratory apparatus during the past  few years, we have attempted to select for listing in this catalog those items of prov- en worth, and for which there is a definite demand on the part of chemists.  It is our stncere belief that the ware listed i n thi s   catalog, manufactured to rigid  specifications under technical supervision, and priced fairly, will continue to merit your  approval, and to conform to the high standards of quality and service we have set for our- selves during the pa.st 22 years   as manufacturers of "PYREX" brand laboratory g1assware.  Your attention is invited to the following features:  1. Descriptions are more complete, more references to the literature have been added, and  the index is more comprehensive.  2 . Practically all ground joints, stoppers, and stopcocks listed in the catalog are n ow  interchangeable .  3. An enlarged line of "LIFETIME RF;D" volumetric ware; also the new line of ECONOMY Red  hospital ware.  4. The number o f pieces per package on many items has been reduced. With smaller pack - ages, p lus the many additions t o our line, many u sers will be able to avail themselves  of higher quantity discounts.  5. Consumer discounts now apply t o assortments as sma11 as 20 original packages.  6. Practically every item, including those in Part II of the catalog, is now subject to  quantity discounts on assortments of original packages.  7 . Reduced prices on many items. Particular attention is called to price rev1s1ons on  centrifuge tubes, condensers, distilling flasks, T interchangeable ground joints and  connections, separatory funnels, stopcocks, tubes for biochemical and clinical use,  a s wel l as on some of the generally used sizes of test tubes, tubi ng, and rod.  8. The catalog becomes effective August 15, 1938. All ware listed i s available through  your regular laboratory supply dealer.  Acknowledgment on the A.tt~ched postage free card o f the safe receipt of this catalog  will be greatly appreciated. Please be sure to indicate on the card whether you desire  to be placed on our regular mailing list to receive our literature from time to time.  Very truly yours,  CORNING GLASS WORKS
